â”‚ 8. **Potential Attack Vectors:**                                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    - **FTP (21/tcp):** Vulnerability assessment for the FTP service, including anonymous access check and version-based vulnerabilities.                                                     â”‚
â”‚    - **SSH (22/tcp):** Credential brute force attacks or exploit known vulnerabilities based on the SSH version.                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    - **NetBIOS (139/tcp) and Microsoft-DS (445/tcp):** Scan for SMB vulnerabilities, including misconfigurations, SMBv1 exploits, and potential for lateral movement if access is gained.    â”‚

â”‚ 9. **Next Steps:**                                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Enumerate the FTP and SSH service for software versions and potential misconfigurations.                                                                                                â”‚

â”‚    - Check for default or weak credentials on the exposed services, particularly FTP and SSH.                                                                                                â”‚
